""SELECT [p0].[Id], [p0].[ApplicationId], [p0].[Approvals], [p0].[At], [p0].[CreatedAt], [p0].[CreatedBy], [p0].[Note], [p0].[Status], [a].[Id], [u].[Id], [h].[Id], [h].[ApplicationId], [h].[At], [h].[Note], [h].[Notified], [h].[ProcessId], [h].[UpdatedAt], [h].[UpdatedBy], [a].[Abbreviation], [a].[ApplicationEmail], [a].[Name], [a].[Team], [a].[TeamEmail], [u].[Abbreviation], [u].[Email], [u].[Name]
FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[ApplicationId], [p].[Approvals], [p].[At], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[Note], [p].[Status]
    FROM [dbo].[Process] AS [p]
    ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_0 ROWS ONLY
) AS [p0]
INNER JOIN [dbo].[Application] AS [a] ON [p0].[ApplicationId] = [a].[Id]
INNER JOIN [dbo].[Unit] AS [u] ON [p0].[At] = [u].[Id]

    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[ApplicationId], [p].[Approvals], [p].[At], [p].[CreatedAt], [p].[CreatedBy], [p].[Note], [p].[Status]
    FROM [dbo].[Process] AS [p]
    ORDER BY [p].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [p0]
INNER JOIN [dbo].[Application] AS [a] ON [p0].[ApplicationId] = [a].[Id]
INNER JOIN [dbo].[Unit] AS [u] ON [p0].[At] = [u].[Id]
LEFT JOIN [History] AS [h] ON [p0].[Id] = [h].[ProcessId]
ORDER BY [p0].[CreatedAt] DESC, [p0].[Id], [a].[Id], [u].[Id]"
